*Grade 1 Maths — November Quiz*
_1703 questions (1203 new + 500 revision)_

*Q1.* ⚖️ Kabir puts a cement bag and a sheet of paper on a seesaw.
A) A sheet of paper
B) Same weight
C) A cement bag
D) Cannot say
✅ *Answer:* C) A cement bag
💡 A cement bag is heavier than a sheet of paper.
━━━━━━━━━━
